<p><a href = vnd.unilang:unknown.html>Unknown</a> <span class="defdate">[<a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> 1821]</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:but.html>but</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:probably.html>probably</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> imitative <a href = vnd.unilang:origin.html>origin</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>compare</a> dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">squacco</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">small-crested <a href = vnd.unilang:heron.html>heron</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stael</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stāl</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*stahal</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stahlą</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:staar.html>staar</a> (8536)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:staar.html>staar</a></strong>
</p>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stat.html>stat</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:stat.html>stat</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stedi</i> (whence <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:steden.html>stede</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">stee</i>), <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stadiz</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*stéh₂tis</i>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> plural <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> preserved <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>old</a> Germanic <a href = vnd.unilang:umlaut.html>umlaut</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> morphological <a href = vnd.unilang:function.html>function</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> rarity <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:several.html>Several</a> derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:have.html>have</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:umlaut.html>umlaut</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:as.html>as</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:well.html>well</a>.
